sniffer dog (‘isnifar) n. [informal] eey uriya daroogada. sniffle (‘isnifal) v. 1 fiiqlayn, siiba cabbur. 2 ooyid, siiba fiiqlayn. e.g. She kept on sniffling all night.

-n. san-fiiqle, siiba cabbur. -sniffler (‘isniflar) n.; -sniffly (‘isnifli) adj.

sniffy (‘isnifi) adj. sniffier, sniffiest. [informal] xaqiraad ama santaag. -sniffily (‘isnifali) adv.; -sniffiness n. snifter (‘isnftar) n. koob madax gunbursan iyo daba dhuuban leh oo khamri lagu dhamo.

snifter

snip (isnip) snipped, snipping. jarid, siiba maqas ku baar goyn. e.g. She snipped my mustache.

-n. 1 jaridyo; hufyo. e.g. With a few snips she cut out my hair. 2 huluf ama cad, siiba wax jarmo ku yimid. e.g. Clean the snips of papers from the floor. 3 snips, maqas, siiba mid biraha jara.

4. snips snipe

snipe (isnaayp) n., pl. snipes. shinbir qaldheer oo ku nool biya-baxooyinka.

-v., sniped, sniping. 1 toogatin, siiba qof meel fog jooga. e.g. The insurgents in the buildings sniped us. 2 cilaaqid; weerarid, siiba hadal. e.g. The mayor sniped the gover nor. -sniper n.

snippy (‘isnipi) adj. snippier, snippiest. [informal] ka kanaan ama xanaq ku jiro. e.g. The teacher was quite snippy when we came late. -snippily (‘isnipali) adv.; - snippiness n.

snitch (isniij) v. [informal] 1 xadid; dhiitin; siibid. 2 sheegid; digid; wargalin qof.

-n. sheege; dige.

snivel (‘isnival) v. sniveled, sniveling. 1 ooyid, siiba fiiq fiiqlayn. 2 cabatin, siiba calaacalid. e.g. She sniveled about her punishment.

-n. fiiq-fiiqlaynyo, siiba oohin yar. -sniveler n.; - snivelingly adv.

snob (isnaab) n. 1 qab-wayni; isla-wayni, siiba qof isgeeya meel uu san gaarsanayn. 2 qof iska dhiga wax uu gaar uga helo in u uu uga sarreeyo dadka kale. e.g. He's a musical snob. -snobbery n. -snobbism n.; -snobby adj. (snobbier, snobbiest).

SNOBOL (‘isnaw,bool) n. luuqad-sare oo kambuyuutar. snoop (isnuup) n. [informal] 1 baarid ama san-la-galid qof kale arrimihiis. e.g. She likes to snoop in my affairs. 2 baare, siiba danbi-baare. -snooper n.; -snoopy adj.

snoot snuck923

snoot (isnuut) n. 1 [informal] sanka qof. 2 [informal] santaage, siiba kibir iyo isla wayni

snooty (‘isnuudhi) adj. snootier, snootiest. [informal] muujiya kibir ama diiddo. -snootily (‘isnuudhali) adv.; -snootiness n.

snooze (isnuuz) n. [informal] gamaanyo; hurdo gaaban, siiba mid maalmeed; indhacasaysi.

-v., snoozed, snoozing. gamaanyood; indhacasyasad. e.g. The deer snoozed on the grass in the sun. -snoozer n.; -snoozy adj. (snoozier, snooziest).

snooze button n. meel laga riixo saacad hurdo oo toosisay qof si uu xoogaa hurdo ah u siihelo.

snore (isnoor) n. 1 khuuro. 2 [informal] wax laga caajiso. -v., snored, snoring. khuurin. e.g. My wife snored all night. -snorer n.

snoring

snorkel (‘isnoorkal) n. dhuun qof biyo ku jira sanka ku xirto oo ka neefsado.

snorkel and mask snorkeler

snort (isnoorti) n. 1 fiifyo, siiba qof wax diiddan. e.g. She gave a snort of disapproval. 2 biifyo; fuufyo, siiba xoolo dareen galo ama wax diida. e.g. The bull gave a snort.

-v. 1 diidid, siiba fiifalayn. e.g. He snored at my idea. 2 biifid; fuuflayn, siiba xoolo. e.g. She ran when the horse snorted. 3 [informal] san-ka-fiiqsad daroogo. snot (isnat) n. [informal] duuf.

snot-nosed adj. [informal] duufle ah, siiba qof yar oo aan waaya-arag ahayn.

snot rag n. [informal] calal-duufeed; masar santiryo. snotty (‘isnaadhi) adj. snottier, snottiest. [informal] 1 duuf leh. 2 qab-wayni muujiya. -snottily adv.; -snottines n. snotty-nosed adj. [informal] la mid snot-nosed. snout (isnawt) n. gafuur dhuuban leh; san iyo qal dheer leh, siiba xoolo. -snouted adj.; -snouty adj. snow (isnaw) n. 1 baraf. 2 shucaac, siiba mid telefishin. -v. 1 di'id baraf. e.g. It's snowing all night. 2 be snowed in, xannibaad baraf keenay. e.g. We were snowed in four days. 3 [informal] faanin, siiba been ah. -snowless adj.; -snowlike adj.

snowball (‘isnaw,bool) n. 1 kuus-barafeed; baraf la kuus kuusay. 2 wax dhaqso u bata.

rolling snowball snowblowing

-v. 1 isku-tuur-tuurid baraf la kuus-kuusay. 2 badatin. snowblower (‘isnaw,balawar) n. baraf-buufshe; qalab banneeya baraf tuurma.

snowboard (‘isnaw,boordh) n. loox-baraf, siiba mid looga taraaraxo baraf goglan. -snowboarding n.

snow boot n. kaba-barafeed.

snowbound (‘isnaw,bawndh) adj. 1 bandaw la saaro aadidda ama ku safridda baraf. 2 baraf qariyo ama go'doonshay. e.g. A small bounded village.

snowcap (‘isnaw,kaap) n. baraf doboola dhakada buur. - snow-capped adj.

snoow chains plural n. silisbarafeed, siiba lagu xiro lug gaari si ay dhulbarafeedka u xagsato.

snowdrift (‘isnaw,dhirifti) n. baraf dabayli buurtay. snowfall (‘isnaw,fool) n. 1 baraf-dhacyo; baraf-da'yo. e.g. Heavy snowfall made driving impossible. 2 baraf intiisa da'day. e.g. The snowfall in last night was 12 inches. snowfield (‘isnaw,fiildh) n. dhul ballaaran oo baraf joogto u yaal.

snowflake (‘isnaw,faleyk) n. xanbuufo-baraf oo duulduusha.

snowflakes

snow gun n. makiinad samaysa baraf samays ah. snow job n. [informal] dhagar, siiba maldahan. snow machine n. magac kale oo loo yaqaan snowmobile. snowman (‘isnaw,maan) n., pl. -men. baraf la dhoodhoobay oo qof loo ekaysiiyay.

snowman

snowmelt (‘isnaw,melti) n. milan-baraf; baraf dhalaalay. snowmobile (‘isnawmaw,biil) n. gaari-barafeed, siiba mid hor ku leh loox taraaraxa iyo lugo danbe.

snowmobile

snowplow (‘isnaw,pilaw) n. baraf-xaare, siiba gaadiid baanneeya waddooyinka.

snowshoe

snowstorm (‘isnaw,istorm) n. baraf culus oo dhaca, siiba mid wata dabayl.

snow tire n. lugo gaari oo leh girgirro barafka qabsada. snow-white adj. midab caddaan saafi ah.

snowy (‘isnawi) adj. snowier, snowiest. 1 baraf saaranyahay; baraf fuulay. e.g. Snowy tree. 2 cimilo ama xilli baraf leh. e.g. Snowy morning. A snowy December day. 3 midab baraf leh. e.g. My teacher has a snowy hair. -snowily (‘isnawali) adv.; -snowiness n.

Snr. abbr. Senior.

snub (isnab) v. snubbed, snubbing. 1 xumayn; xaqirid; diidid, siiba inkirid. e.g. She snubbed her neighbors. The new leader snubbed his poor relations. 2 xirid, siiba xoolo ama doon. e.g. A camel snubbed to a tree.

-n. xaqiraad, siiba qof la inkiro ama la ceebeeyo. e.g. We were angry by her snub.

-adj. kamas leh [in combination] jirdacan. e.g. Snub-nosed. snubber (‘isnabar) n. raqle-dhime.

snuck (isnak) [informal] past and past participle of sneak.
